<rating>5</rating><username>Jaspery<//username><Resp>None< /Resp><date>1594500916740< /date><gmap_id>0x80dc07333d738cf5:0xeb967863635b63f5<//gmap_id><Review>This was my first time using both packers and movers. I've had to move several times in the past few years and have always done it myself (rented a truck, asked for friends help, etc.). This move would be pretty big one for me and my husband - about two hours away from San Diego, and booking with 1st Choice Movers was the best decision we could have made to make our move so incredibly stress-free! Derek was the one whom we coordinated with and he was always quick to respond and clear with his communication. He was upfront about the cost and the final estimate actually ended up being a bit lower than what he quoted to us originally!

The day before the big move the packing team showed up - Brenda, Lily, and Vanessa. We were informed that they would arrive at 9am, but they were told to come at 8:30am from management - no big deal at all though, just a slight miscommunication (and coming early never hurts!). The three ladies were professional, super nice, and worked quickly. If they had any questions about whether something needed to get packed or not, they didn't hesitate to ask. We're currently in the process of unpacking at our new place, and we have yet to see anything that's broken or damaged. They finished packing up our 1 bedroom apartment in just under 2.5 hours.

The big move was the next day and Alex, Jerzy, and Lalo were the moving team - they showed up right on time. Like the packing team, they were professional and efficient. They were able to load things up in about 2 hours and unload in 1 short hour! My husband and I were amazed at how quick they were. We also did buy them lunch and expected them to take a longer break, but after about 10 minutes of eating they continued working hard. The total move day was about 5.5 hours for us (2 hours to load, 2 hours to drive, a little over 1 hour to unload).

If you have any anxiety about moving, definitely hire this team! They will put you at ease and allow you to have a stress-free move day (which I never thought could be possible before this!). We can't emphasize enough how each team member was extremely professional, efficient, and friendly.

Also, in these times especially (but even during non-pandemic times), if someone does an amazing job and you're pleased with the work - give them a tip! We tipped both of the packers and the movers as we were completely satisfied with their work.</Review></record>

Once we completed the exam I was pleased to hear there will be no procedures that need to be done and he even gave me a referral for my sleep apnea which I've been suffering from for years!

Then back to the front to Gina that once again was very good at finalizing my visit and setting my next appointment.  Overall great experience, who knew going to the dentist would be such an easy and fun experience.  I laughed and had a fun experience when normally it's filled with pain and awkward silence.  Not here...you're constantly in a circle of great people communicating with you and attending to your needs.

I found a dentist office at last.</text>< pics>

<Text>I was extremely impressed by this place. It's kind of like Chipotle but with more authentic Mexican flavor and ingredients. You go through the line to custom build tacos, burritos or bowls. The carne asada and shrimp were delicious and they served chips and salsa along with the meal. They also had some refreshing infused waters and a complete bar.

< text>
Stumbled onto this place accidentally, while looking for another restaurant. It seemed inviting, with multiple patrons dining at tables on the little side patio outdoors. We ordered their individual tacos, which were good-sized, & you get to choose all the ingredients. We had ours loaded with carne asada, rice, black beans, salsa, sour cream, cheese, & more. They were mouth watering! Served with chips & salsa on the side, at no extra charge. They have a variety of meats, including pork & chicken. Loved this place, & we will definitely go back again!<//text>

<Review>The guys came to Livermore for the first time to visit me (I'm always driving down to San Jose to visit them), so I needed to take them somewhere really good. Cinco TacoBar delivered, and even my picky-eater-type friends polished off their burritos. Wow,  Bravo.  Just finished my burrito and it was so good I felt compelled to write a review while I can still taste it. I had carne asada burrito and wife had chicken bowl with guacamole and both were fantastic and made to order to go in front of us. Spicy salsa too! They have a full bar serving mixed drinks which was unexpected due to the small size of the place. Drinks and bar looked very professional. I've been to 30+ Mexican restaurants in the Tri valley and this is instantly now in my top 5. Don't be fooled by small storefront or the old taco bell location,  it has my 2 thumbs up!  Clean stylish dining area too. 6/5 stars for my first visit!</Text>

< review>
I was in a real bind with my phone situation.  My phone was in pieces, no insurance, still owed for the phone, at the time I had been without a phone for 8 days.  I had been to a different Sprint store earlier in the week and also had talked with Customer Care on the phone and both basically had said that I was going to pay $400 + up front to get a new phone.
I walked in and to my surprise there was no wait, Dwayne was prompt to greet me and find out what I was in need of.  I explained my situation and was waiting for the bad news.  But this time I was given an option other than pay a lot out of pocket. He said I could add another line to my plan and get a brand new phone to use.  Although my bill would go up slightly more a month, it beat more than $400.
At this point Alfonso, the Assistant Manager overheard my situation and said he could help even more.  He went above and beyond to make things happen for me.  He got me upgraded to a better plan at not additional cost.  Alfonso got me all set up with a new phone and toys to go with it.

It took some time to get it all done because of my situation and it also required Alfonso to make some calls to Sprint Care in order to get everything in order.  He had no problem taking an hour to get everything perfect and in order.  I know some people walk in the stores and want the sales team to snap their fingers and you are out the door.  But it takes time. (Make an appointment to be safe)
When I fist walked in there was only 1 other guest being helped.  So I got helped right away, I considered myself lucky because I didn't have an appointment.  As guests came in they were promptly greeted and helped.  Caesar and Jordan were both conversing with me about my phone situation but were quick to help the guests as they came into the store.  I will be going back to see this crew whenever I need anything dealing with Sprint.</review>

< Review>
Martin's is both a great place for eating and a great place for volunteering!  The organization is entirely run by volunteers and funded entirely by donations (it receives no city, state, or federal funding.) The food is delicious and largely vegetarian. The service is kind. The garden is beautiful. It is a very special place.< /Review>

< Review>
The people who serve the food are great people who absolutely care about you. Its a family that you never had. I myself was a volunteer for over 4 straight years at a inner Mission district food pantry and hot meals. Its a very valuable experience. I learned how to love all people, no matter where they are from. Martin De Porres has the same volunteers who love all people, because we are all one people, one very large family. By the way they provide showers and toiletries. Call in for more info on times and days for the showers and toiletries.

Thank you,
Adam</Review>

< review>
Not many mexican places are packed on a Sunday at 1pm, but this one was so there must be something about it. To my surprise, I didn't expect that. The menu has a more limited and different offering than a taco shop. It obviously is for breakfast/brunch, and they do a good job at it. I tried the huevos divorciados, and although it is simple, it was quite good. The beans are good, the potatoes on the soft side, but I would have liked the salsas to be a little spicier. Overall, this is a great place to have a mexican brunch.<//review>
